<td style=" text-align: center;margin:auto; vertical-align:top"><span style="font-weight:bold">(Nasdaq Global Select Market)</span></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Indicate by check mark whether the registrant is an emerging growth company as defined in Rule 405 of the Securities Act of 1933 (&#167;230.405 of this chapter) or Rule <span style="white-space:nowrap">12b-2</span> of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934 <span style="white-space:nowrap">(&#167;240.12b-2</span> of this chapter).</p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:right">Emerging growth company&#160;&#160;<ix:nonNumeric name="dei:EntityEmergingGrowthCompany" contextRef="duration_2020-10-22_to_2020-10-22" format="ixt-sec:boolballotbox">&#9744;</ix:nonNumeric></p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If an emerging growth company, indicate by check mark if the registrant has elected not to use the extended transition period for complying with any new or revised financial accounting standards provided pursuant to Section&#160;13(a) of the Exchange Act.&#160;&#160;&#9744;</p> <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p> <p style="line-height:1.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&#160;</p> <p style="line-height:3.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&#160;</p></div></div>

<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Other Events. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On October&#160;22, 2020, the Superior Court of the State of California, County of Santa Clara (the &#8220;Court&#8221;), granted preliminary approval of the settlement of the stockholder derivative action captioned<span style="font-style:italic">&#160;In re Alphabet Inc. Shareholder Derivative Litigation</span>, Lead Case No. 19CV341522, as well as other related litigations pending in the United States District Court for the Northern District of California and the Delaware Court of Chancery and litigation demands made by certain stockholders of the company (collectively, the &#8220;Settled Matters&#8221;). The complaints and demands in the Settled Matters alleged that certain defendants breached their fiduciary duties in connection with (1)&#160;an alleged pattern of sexual harassment and discrimination by male executives at the company and (2)&#160;a data bug, allegedly in violation of state and federal law. The Settled Matters were resolved pursuant to a Stipulation and Agreement of Settlement (the &#8220;Stipulation&#8221;). </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Pursuant to the Court&#8217;s Order granting preliminary approval of the settlement, the company is publishing the Notice of Pendency and Proposed Settlement of Derivative Actions (the &#8220;Notice&#8221;), attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1. The Notice and Stipulation are available for review on the company&#8217;s investor relations website at https://abc.xyz/investor/. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><I><U>This is not a solicitation from a lawyer.</U> </I></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">TO:</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify">ALL PERSONS AND ENTITIES WHO HELD ALPHABET INC. COMMON STOCK AS OF THE CLOSE OF TRADING ON AUGUST&nbsp;20,
2020 </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>PLEASE READ THIS NOTICE CAREFULLY AND IN ITS ENTIRETY.</B> This Notice relates to a proposed
settlement (&#147;<B>Settlement</B>&#148;) of the following derivative actions: <I>In re Alphabet Inc. Shareholder Derivative Litigation</I>, Lead Case No. 19CV341522 (Cal. Super. Ct., Cnty. of Santa Clara) (&#147;<B>California Action</B>&#148;);
<I>Irving Firemen&#146;s Relief</I><I></I><I>&nbsp;&amp; Ret. Fund v. Page</I>, C.A. No. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2019-0355-SG</FONT> (Del. Ch.) (the &#147;<B>Delaware Action</B>&#148;); <I>Bao v. Page</I>, Case No.: <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">4:19-cv-00314-JSW</FONT></FONT></FONT> (N.D. Cal.); <I>Cordeiro v. Page</I>, Case No.: <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">4:19-cv-01063-JSW</FONT></FONT></FONT> (N.D. Cal.); <I>Green v. Page</I>,<I> </I>Case No.: <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT

proposed Settlement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">All capitalized terms used in this Notice that are not otherwise defined herein have the meanings
provided in the Stipulation and Agreement of Settlement entered into on August 20, 2020 (&#147;<B>Stipulation</B>&#148;), by and among (a)&nbsp;Northern California Pipe Trades Pension Plan (&#147;<B>NCPTPP</B>&#148;), Teamsters Local 272 Labor
Management Pension Fund (&#147;<B>Local 272</B>&#148;), James Martin, LR Trust, Jonathan Reiss, Allen Wiesenfeld, Sjunde <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">AP-Fonden</FONT> (&#147;<B>AP7</B>&#148;), John R. O&#146;Neil, Jackson D. Morgus, Victor Bao,
Daniel Cordeiro, Scott Galbiati, Ian Green, Leo Shumacher, Steve Sims, Joseph Lipovich, Esther Schlafrig, D.M. Cohen, Inc., Erste Asset Management, Irving Firemen&#146;s Relief&nbsp;&amp; Retirement Fund (&#147;<B>Irving Fire</B>&#148;), Karen
Sbriglio, and Roger Morrell (collectively, the &#147;<B>Settling Stockholders</B>&#148;); (b) Nominal Defendant Alphabet Inc. (&#147;<B>Alphabet</B>&#148; or the &#147;<B>Company</B>&#148;), by and through the Special Litigation Committee
(&#147;<B>SLC</B>&#148;) of Alphabet&#146;s Board of Directors; and (c)&nbsp;Lawrence E. Page, Sergey Brin, Eric E. Schmidt, Sundar Pichai, John L. Hennessy, L. John Doerr, Kavitark Ram Shriram, Alan R. Mulally, Ann Mather, Roger W. Ferguson, Jr.,
Diane B. Greene, Shirley M. Tilghman, Robin L. Washington, Andrew E. Rubin, Amit Singhal, Laszlo Bock, David C. Drummond, Eileen Naughton, and Ruth E. Porat (collectively, the &#147;<B>Individual Defendants</B>&#148; and, together with Alphabet,
&#147;<B>Defendants</B>,&#148; and, together with the Settling Stockholders, the &#147;<B>Settling Parties</B>&#148;). </P>

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>THIS NOTICE PROVIDES ONLY A SUMMARY OF THE MATERIAL TERMS OF THE
SETTLEMENT AND RELEASES. </B>You can obtain more information by reviewing the Stipulation, which is available on Plaintiffs&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Counsel&#146;s websites at <FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" COLOR="#0000ff"><U>https://www.bottinilaw.com</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman"> and
</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" COLOR="#0000ff"><U>https://www.cohenmilstein.com</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman">, and on Alphabet&#146;s investor relations website at </FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" COLOR="#0000ff"><U>https://abc.xyz/investor/</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman">. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">Because the Settlement involves the resolution of derivative actions, which were brought on behalf of and for the benefit of
the Company, the benefits from the Settlement will go to Alphabet. Individual Alphabet stockholders will not receive any direct payment from the Settlement.<B> ACCORDINGLY, THERE IS NO PROOF OF CLAIM FORM FOR STOCKHOLDERS TO SUBMIT IN CONNECTION
WITH THIS SETTLEMENT. </B> </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P><DIV ALIGN="right">
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="99%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">


<TR>

<TD WIDTH="100%"></TD></TR>


<TR STYLE="font-size:1pt">
<TD HEIGHT="8" STYLE="BORDER-LEFT:1px solid #000000; BORDER-TOP:1px solid #000000; BORDER-RIGHT:1px solid #000000; padding-left:8pt" BGCOLOR="#e6e6e6">&nbsp;</TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">
<TD VALIGN="bottom" ALIGN="center" STYLE="padding-bottom:6pt ;BORDER-LEFT:1px solid #000000; BORDER-RIGHT:1px solid #000000; BORDER-BOTTOM:1px solid #000000; padding-left:8pt; padding-right:2pt" BGCOLOR="#e6e6e6">WHAT IS THE PURPOSE OF THIS
NOTICE?</TD></TR>
</TABLE></DIV> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The purpose of this Notice is to
explain the Settled Matters, the terms of the proposed Settlement of those litigations and stockholder litigation demands, and how the proposed Settlement affects Alphabet stockholders&#146; legal rights. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Superior Court of the State of California for the County of Santa Clara
(&#147;<B>California State Court</B>&#148; or the &#147;<B>Court</B>&#148;) will hold a hearing (&#147;<B>Settlement Hearing</B>&#148;) on November&nbsp;30, 2020, at 1:30 p.m., at the Superior Court of the State of California, County of Santa Clara,
Dept. 1, 191 North First Street, San Jose, CA 95113, at which the Court will consider whether the Judgment, substantially in the form of Exhibit D to the Stipulation, should be entered: (a)&nbsp;approving the terms of the Settlement as fair,
reasonable, and adequate, and in the best interests of Alphabet and Alphabet&#146;s stockholders; (b)&nbsp;dismissing with prejudice the California Action pursuant to the terms of this Stipulation; and (c)&nbsp;ruling upon Settling
Stockholders&#146; Counsel&#146;s (other than Delaware Counsel) application for a Fee&nbsp;&amp; Expense Award; and (d)&nbsp;to consider any other matters that may properly be brought before the Court in connection with the Settlement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Delaware Court of Chancery (the &#147;<B>Delaware Court</B>&#148;) will
hold a separate hearing on December&nbsp;23, 2020 at 10:00 a.m., at 34 The Circle, Georgetown, DE 19947, at which the Delaware Court will rule upon Delaware Counsel&#146;s application for a Fee&nbsp;&amp; Expense Award (the &#147;<B>Delaware Fee
Hearing</B>&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P><DIV ALIGN="right">
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="99%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">


<TR>

<TD WIDTH="100%"></TD></TR>


<TR STYLE="font-size:1pt">

<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">
<TD VALIGN="bottom" ALIGN="center" STYLE="padding-bottom:6pt ;BORDER-LEFT:1px solid #000000; BORDER-RIGHT:1px solid #000000; BORDER-BOTTOM:1px solid #000000; padding-left:8pt; padding-right:2pt" BGCOLOR="#e6e6e6">WHAT IS THIS CASE ABOUT? WHAT HAS
HAPPENED SO FAR?</TD></TR>
</TABLE></DIV> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">THE FOLLOWING DESCRIPTION OF THE ACTION AND THE SETTLEMENT HAS BEEN PREPARED BY COUNSEL FOR THE SETTLING
PARTIES. THE COURT HAS MADE NO FINDINGS WITH RESPECT TO SUCH MATTERS, AND THIS NOTICE IS NOT AN EXPRESSION OR STATEMENT BY THE COURT OF FINDINGS OF FACT. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>A.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify"><B>Factual Background </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Settlement arises out of the Litigations, as well as the Demands,
alleging breaches of fiduciary duties, among other claims, against certain officers and directors of the Company. Settling Stockholders alleged in their Litigations and Demands that the Individual Defendants breached their fiduciary duties in
connection with (1)&nbsp;an alleged pattern of sexual harassment and discrimination by high-powered male executives at the Company and (2)&nbsp;a data bug, allegedly in violation of state and federal law, including a consent decree with the Federal
Trade Commission, and Alphabet&#146;s own code of conduct. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Among other
things, Settling Stockholders alleged that Alphabet&#146;s Board of Directors (the &#147;<B>Board</B>&#148;) and the Company&#146;s senior executives improperly awarded multi-million-dollar severance packages to several male executives accused of
sexually harassing female employees, even after internal investigations determined those accusations to be credible. For example, Settling Stockholders alleged that in 2014, an internal investigation confirmed allegations of sexual harassment
against Defendant Rubin. Settling Stockholders alleged that following an internal investigation, the LDCC approved a $90&nbsp;million severance package for Defendant Rubin. Settling Stockholders also alleged that when Defendant Singhal resigned in
2016, after an internal investigation found credible an allegation of sexual harassment, the LDCC improperly approved a $45&nbsp;million severance package for Singhal. Settling Stockholders alleged in their Litigations and Demands that these actions
and payouts were part of a broader discriminatory culture that resulted in alleged discrimination against women by, among other things, assigning women jobs in lower compensation &#147;bands&#148; than similarly situated men, promoting women more
slowly and at lower rates than similarly situated men, and paying women less. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Certain of the Settling Stockholders alleged in their respective Litigations
or Demands that certain Individual Defendants breached their fiduciary duties by concealing from regulators and the public a bug in the Google+ social networking platform that was operated by the Company&#146;s subsidiary, Google LLC
(&#147;<B>Google</B>&#148;), which meant that certain applications may have had access to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-public</FONT> Google+ data for an approximately three-year period. Certain of those Settled Matters also alleged that the
data bug led to a consumer class action lawsuit against Google (which was settled for $7.5&nbsp;million and is pending final court approval). Certain Settling Stockholders separately alleged that on January&nbsp;21, 2019, the French data protection
authority fined Google approximately $57&nbsp;million for allegedly breaching the European Union&#146;s data privacy law (which is pending appeal). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">7.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Individual Defendants deny the allegations made by the Settling
Stockholders in the Litigations and Demands. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>B.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify"><B>Procedural History in the California Action </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">8.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On January&nbsp;9, 2019, Plaintiffs NCPTPP and Local 272 filed a stockholder
derivative action in San Mateo Court against certain of the Individual Defendants. On January&nbsp;10, 2019, Plaintiff Martin also filed a stockholder derivative action against certain of the Individual Defendants in San Mateo Court. Prior to filing
suit, Plaintiff Martin had propounded a stockholder inspection demand on the Company and had received a production of books and records from the Company, relevant portions of which were included in Plaintiff Martin&#146;s complaint, which was filed
under seal. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">3 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">9.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On January&nbsp;24, 2019,
a related complaint was filed in the California State Court by Plaintiffs LR Trust, Jonathan Reiss, and Allen Wiesenfeld. In an effort to coordinate the pending actions, on February&nbsp;14, 2019, the <I>Martin</I> and <I>N.&nbsp;Cal. Pipe
Trades</I> actions were transferred to the California State Court from San Mateo Court. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">10.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On February&nbsp;22, 2019, Plaintiffs Martin, NCPTPP, and Local 272 filed a
motion with the California State Court to consolidate the <I>Martin</I>, <I>N. Cal. Pipe Trades</I>, and <I>LR Trust</I> actions, appoint themselves as lead plaintiffs, and to appoint Bottini&nbsp;&amp; Bottini and Cohen Milstein as <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-lead</FONT> counsel (&#147;<B>Motion to Consolidate and Appoint Lead Counsel</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">11.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On March&nbsp;19, 2019, a related complaint was filed in the California
State Court by Plaintiff AP7, after first making a litigation demand on the Board and having received a production of books and records from the Company in response to a stockholder inspection demand. On March&nbsp;22, 2019, Plaintiff AP7 filed a
response to the Motion to Consolidate and Appoint Lead Counsel, requesting that the <I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">AP-Fonden</FONT></I> complaint be maintained separately through the demurrer stage. In addition, on April&nbsp;30 2019,
Plaintiffs the New York City Employees&#146; Retirement System, the Teachers&#146; Retirement System of the City of New York, the New York City Fire Department Pension Fund, Subchapter 2, and the New York City Board of Education Retirement System
(collectively, the &#147;<B>NYC Funds</B>&#148;) filed a related complaint in California State Court, and voluntarily dismissed an action they had filed in the Delaware Court on May&nbsp;1, 2019 after refiling in the California State Court. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">12.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On May&nbsp;10, 2019, the California State Court held a hearing on the
Motion to Consolidate and Appoint Lead Counsel and responses and replies thereto by Plaintiffs AP7 and the NYC Funds. The hearing was attended by all counsel for the applicable parties and extensive oral argument was presented to the California
State Court. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">13.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On May&nbsp;16, 2019, the California State Court ordered
that the <I>Martin</I>, <I>Pipe Trades</I>, <I>LR Trust</I>, <I>AP7</I>, and <I>NYC Funds</I> actions be consolidated for all purposes;<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> and appointed NCPTPP, Local 272, and Martin as <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs and Bottini&nbsp;&amp; Bottini, Inc. and Cohen Milstein Sellers&nbsp;&amp; Toll PLLC as Plaintiffs&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Counsel, with the exception that Plaintiff
AP7 be allowed to maintain a separate complaint and its counsel would serve as counsel of its own case through the demurrer stage. The Order anticipated that, in the event of settlement discussions, AP7 would participate in such discussions with
Alphabet and the SLC. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">14.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On August&nbsp;16, 2019, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs filed a consolidated complaint in the California Action, asserting four claims: (1)&nbsp;breach of fiduciary duty; (2)&nbsp;unjust enrichment; (3)&nbsp;corporate waste; and (4)&nbsp;abuse of
control (<I>In re Alphabet Inc. S&#146;holder Deriv. Litig.</I>, Lead Case No. 19CV341522; the &#147;<B>Consolidated Complaint</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">15.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On February&nbsp;18, 2020, Jackson D. Morgus filed a related complaint in
California State Court. On March&nbsp;18, 2020, John R. O&#146;Neil filed a related complaint in California State Court. On May&nbsp;20, 2020, the California State Court ordered that the <I>Morgus</I> and <I>O&#146;Neil</I> actions be consolidated
into the California Action. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="line-height:8.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;width:27%">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> On November&nbsp;12, 2019, the NYC Funds stipulated to the dismissal of
their complaint from the Consolidated Action, and the California State Court granted that dismissal without prejudice on November&nbsp;15, 2019. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">4 </P>

</DIV></Center>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>C.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify"><B>The Federal Actions </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">16.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Federal Actions were commenced between January&nbsp;18, 2019 and
March&nbsp;11, 2019 by Plaintiffs Bao, Cordeiro, Galbiati, Green, Sims, Shumacher, and Lipovich, asserting claims for breach of fiduciary duty, corporate waste, unjust enrichment and violations of the federal securities laws. The claims in the
Federal Actions arise out of alleged misconduct of certain current and former employees, approval of severance payments, privacy concerns including with regard to a bug in the Google+ social networking platform and related statements and omissions.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">17.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Prior to filing suit, Plaintiffs Green, Sims, Shumacher and Lipovich
had propounded a stockholder inspection demand on the Company and had received a production of books and records from the Company, relevant portions of which were cited in their complaints. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">18.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Thereafter, counsel for plaintiffs prepared motions to consolidate the five
cases and to appoint Robbins LLP as lead counsel for plaintiffs in the Federal Actions. Plaintiffs in the Federal Actions also filed briefs in opposition to Defendants&#146; motions to stay the Federal Actions. Defendants&#146; motion was granted on
February&nbsp;5, 2020, and the Federal Actions were stayed pending resolution of the California Action. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>D.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify"><B>The Delaware Action </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">19.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On May&nbsp;14, 2019, Plaintiff Irving Fire filed the Delaware Action in
the Delaware Court. Before filing suit, Irving Fire had propounded a stockholder inspection demand on the Company and had received a production of documents from the Company. Relying on those documents, it filed a complaint under seal. The Delaware
Action, like the California Action and Federal Actions, contains allegations regarding alleged misconduct by certain current and former employees, approval of severance payments, and privacy concerns including with regard to a bug in the Google+
social networking platform and related statements and omissions. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">20.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On
June&nbsp;14, 2019, Defendants filed a Motion to Stay or Dismiss the Delaware Action arguing that the Delaware Action should be stayed (or, alternatively, dismissed) in favor of the California Action. Defendants&#146; motion was briefed and
thereafter denied by the Delaware Court on July&nbsp;1, 2019 after argument. On July&nbsp;22, 2019, the SLC filed a Motion to Stay the Delaware Action pending completion of the SLC&#146;s process, which motion was briefed, argued and thereafter
granted by the Delaware Court on September&nbsp;6, 2019. The parties agreed to extend the stay of the Delaware Action while the parties engaged in mediation. The stay is currently in place. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>E.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify"><B>The Demands </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">21.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;From February 2019 to June 2019, the Board received the six Demands. The
Demands were sent by stockholders AP7, Esther Schlafrig, D.M. Cohen, Inc., Karen Sbriglio, Erste Asset Management GmbH, and Roger Morrell. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">5 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>F.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify"><B>The Special Litigation Committee </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">22.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Prior to the filing of the Litigations and the submission of the Demands,
the Company&#146;s Board established a Special Committee on November&nbsp;28, 2018 to oversee a comprehensive review by management of company policies and processes related to sexual harassment and/or sexual misconduct (including those related to
investigations into allegations of sexual harassment and/or sexual misconduct and subsequent decision-making processes regarding termination and severance). The Company retained Wilmer Cutler Pickering Hale and Dorr LLP
(&#147;<B>WilmerHale</B>&#148;) to conduct this review, which included, among other things, a thorough analysis of existing policies, reporting channels, investigatory practices and procedures, disciplinary and remedial practices, training and
education, and monitoring and oversight. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">23.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On February&nbsp;28, 2019,
the Board unanimously approved draft resolutions forming a special litigation committee to consider the derivative lawsuits on file and related litigation demands, as well as any similar, subsequent derivative suits or demand letters. The Board
ratified the final resolutions appointing the SLC on April&nbsp;24, 2019. The SLC is composed of two outside directors, Roger Ferguson and Ann Mather, who the Board determined in appointing them are in all respects independent and disinterested with
respect to the Demands and Litigations. The SLC retained Cravath, Swaine&nbsp;&amp; Moore LLP (&#147;<B>Cravath</B>&#148;) and Abrams&nbsp;&amp; Bayliss LLP to serve as its independent counsel. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">24.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The SLC assumed oversight of the comprehensive review of policies and
processes, previously overseen by the Special Committee, and expanded the scope of that review to include policies and processes related to anti-retaliation and pay equity. That review included an examination of relevant documents, including company
policies, procedures and guidance and training materials, as well as interviews of company employees. Cravath and the SLC independently considered and assessed the process and findings of the review, as well as a set of recommended enhancements that
resulted from it. After deliberation, the SLC approved the proposed enhancements. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">25.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The SLC was also given the full authority of the Board to evaluate the
allegations and claims asserted in the Demands and in the Litigations, and to arrive at such decisions and take such actions in connection with the Demands and Litigations that the SLC deemed appropriate and in the best interests of the Company and
its stockholders, including, without limitation, deciding whether to pursue such claims, to seek a consensual resolution or to seek dismissal. The SLC completed a thorough and independent investigation beginning in approximately May 2019 and
substantially concluding in December 2019,<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> during which, Cravath, at the direction of the SLC, reviewed emails from multiple custodians, Board and Board committee materials, and relevant company
documents, and interviewed current and former Alphabet directors and company employees. Cravath regularly reported to the SLC during the course of its work, meeting with the SLC, either in person or by telephone, sixteen times between May 2019 and
January 2020 (and subsequently in connection with this Settlement). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">26.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On
December&nbsp;9, 2019, the SLC, through Cravath, responded by letter to counsel for all parties to the Demands and Litigations that it had completed its investigation of the </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="line-height:8.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;width:25%">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> A stay of the proceedings in the Delaware Action until December&nbsp;13, 2019, and an extension for Defendants to respond to the operative complaints in the California Action until the same date,
enabled the SLC to conduct an unencumbered investigation. The stay/response dates in both actions have since been extended to accommodate the mediation process. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">6 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">
allegations and claims asserted in the Demands and Litigations. Cravath informed counsel that based on its investigation, the SLC had determined that &#147;it [wa]s in the best interests of the
Company and its stockholders for the parties, including the demanding stockholders, to attempt to resolve the claims through a global mediation.&#148; The SLC reached that conclusion based on its analysis that the claims asserted were not in the
best interests of Alphabet to pursue. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>G.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify"><B>The Litigation Progress and Extensive Settlement Negotiations </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">27.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Prior to the filing of the Consolidated Complaint in the California Action,
Plaintiffs&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Counsel reviewed 1,900 pages of internal documents produced by Alphabet in response to Lead Plaintiffs&#146; stockholder inspection demands. Prior to making its litigation demand and
filing its complaint, AP7 also reviewed internal documents that Alphabet produced in response to AP7&#146;s stockholder inspection demand. Delaware Counsel reviewed internal documents produced by Alphabet in response to Irving Fire&#146;s
stockholder inspection demand before filing the Delaware Action. These documents included, among other things, (1)&nbsp;minutes, agendas, board packages, communications, and other materials relating to regularly conducted and special meetings of the
Board and the LDCC; (2)&nbsp;internal company policies, including Code of Conduct and Relationships with Coworkers and Employment of Relatives Policy, and drafts thereof; (3)&nbsp;employment and termination agreements of certain executives; and
(4)&nbsp;certain director and officer questionnaires. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">28.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Settling
Stockholders&#146; Counsel engaged in extensive settlement negotiations with Defendants spanning many months. The settlement negotiations were conducted under the auspices of the Hon. James P. Kleinberg (Ret.). Prior to commencing the formal
settlement negotiations, in order to more fully inform themselves of all relevant facts, Plaintiffs&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Counsel attended several <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-person</FONT> as well as
telephonic/video conferences with counsel for the Alphabet Defendants and the SLC. For example, on January&nbsp;14, 2020, Plaintiffs&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Counsel, along with Louise Renne and Ann Ravel, met in person
with counsel for the Alphabet Defendants, certain Alphabet representatives, and WilmerHale in Mountain View, California and Washington, D.C. At the meeting, WilmerHale provided an extensive presentation regarding the Company&#146;s corporate
governance practices and internal controls on issues relevant to the allegations in the Litigations and the Demands and an Alphabet representative gave a presentation on Google&#146;s privacy program, including the growth and development of certain
policies and processes as well as a discussion of privacy training for employees and privacy tools for users. Alphabet also produced relevant policies and procedures. Separately, AP7&#146;s counsel and expert met with Cravath in person on
September&nbsp;20, 2019. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">29.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Delaware Counsel participated in multiple
telephonic conferences with counsel for the Alphabet Defendants and Cravath before commencing formal settlement negotiations. Delaware Counsel&#146;s communications with Cravath included a letter raising additional factual allegations on
October&nbsp;10, 2019, telephonic discussions regarding the SLC&#146;s investigation on September&nbsp;10 and October&nbsp;15, 2019, as well as subsequent email <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">check-ins.</FONT> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">30.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On January&nbsp;17, 2020, to ensure the Settling Parties had adequate
information for the mediation, the SLC, through Cravath, made a detailed oral presentation to counsel for the Settling Parties regarding the SLC&#146;s investigation process and findings. The presentation lasted several hours and included an oral
summary of the SLC&#146;s investigation, findings and conclusions, including review of certain internal Company documents, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-mails,</FONT> and Board and LDCC minutes,
</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">7 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">
which had been circulated to the Settling Parties in advance. In addition to Cravath summarizing the SLC&#146;s findings with respect to Google&#146;s user data privacy program, the presentation
also included a description by WilmerHale of relevant policies and procedures related to harassment, retaliation and pay equity, as well as a discussion of the workplace enhancements that the SLC had approved and adopted for inclusion in any
resolution. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">31.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Following receipt and review of this information, Settling
Stockholders&#146; Counsel engaged in a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">two-day</FONT> mediation with Defendants&#146; counsel on January&nbsp;22, 2020 and January&nbsp;23, 2020. Judge Kleinberg served as the mediator, and the mediation sessions
were held in San Francisco at JAMS&#146; offices. At the mediation, to streamline the negotiations and make them more effective, Judge Kleinberg appointed two working groups, consisting of Company counsel and counsel for the Alphabet Defendants
(&#147;<B>Defendants&#146; Working Group</B>&#148;) and representatives of the Settling Stockholders&#146; Counsel: Plaintiffs&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Counsel (Frank Bottini and Julie Goldsmith Reiser), Louise Renne,
and Ann Ravel (&#147;<B>California Plaintiffs&#146; Working Group</B>&#148;). The California Plaintiffs&#146; Working Group and Defendants&#146; Working Group had several meetings, in between which the California Plaintiffs&#146; Working Group kept
other Settling Stockholders&#146; Counsel apprised of developments and sought their input in negotiating the settlement terms. Separately, Delaware Counsel discussed with Defendants&#146; Working Group a set of proposed workplace initiatives,
communicated by Delaware Counsel to Defendants&#146; counsel and the SLC on February&nbsp;20, 2020, and corporate governance enhancements, communicated by Delaware Counsel to Defendants&#146; counsel and the SLC on February&nbsp;21, 2020. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">32.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The California Plaintiffs&#146; Working Group and Defendants&#146; Working
Group also met, in person, on February&nbsp;25, 2020 in Palo Alto, California to further discuss a potential settlement. Judge Kleinberg also attended and facilitated the parties&#146; discussions. During this time, Plaintiffs&#146; <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Counsel also consulted with their retained experts on numerous matters relevant to the pending litigation and the settlement issues, including a corporate governance expert and a data privacy expert, and
provided feedback on the proposed Settlement Consideration. Delaware Counsel and Defendants&#146; counsel also exchanged offers and counter offers on the proposed Settlement Consideration. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">33.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;During the ensuing further settlement discussions, the Settling Parties
affirmed the appropriateness of the workplace enhancements adopted by the SLC, and agreed to revisions to certain recommendations originally proposed as part of the SLC Review. The Settling Parties also reached agreement on the additional governance
reforms reflected in the Stipulation. In addition, after Alphabet agreed to establish the Diversity, Equity and Inclusion Advisory Council as part of the settlement negotiations (the &#147;<B>DEI Advisory Council</B>&#148;), the California
Plaintiffs&#146; Working Group researched, interviewed, and advocated for numerous persons to serve on the DEI Advisory Council who they believed would help the DEI Advisory Council achieve its goals. The California Plaintiffs&#146; Working Group
relayed their recommendations to Defendants&#146; Working Group and had many calls and discussions regarding the membership of the Council, its relationship with the LDCC and Board, and other matters relevant to the governance reforms. These
discussions involved dozens of calls, meetings, and communications over a three-month time period, during which the parties exchanged numerous offers and counter-offers regarding different elements of the proposed settlement. Delaware Counsel and
counsel for the Alphabet Defendants also engaged in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">follow-up</FONT> discussions following the second mediation. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">8 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">34.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Cravath, as counsel for
the SLC, attended the first <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">two-day</FONT> mediation session in person (and was available by phone for the third day), reviewed all settlement demands and proposals sent by all the Settling Parties, and discussed the
evolving negotiations with, and sought feedback from, the SLC. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">35.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On
April&nbsp;20, 2020, Plaintiffs&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Counsel, Delaware Counsel, and counsel for the Alphabet Defendants negotiated a Memorandum of Understanding (&#147;<B>MOU</B>&#148;), which was executed by the
Settling Parties (other than Sbriglio). Following negotiations, counsel for the Alphabet Defendants and counsel for Sbriglio reached agreement on certain aspects of the Settlement Consideration. Counsel for Sbriglio subsequently joined in the
Settlement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">36.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Following the agreement in principle to settle, counsel
for the Alphabet Defendants and the SLC produced to Plaintiffs&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Counsel certain information in order to ensure that the Settlement was fair, adequate, and reasonable and in the best interests of
the Settling Stockholders and Alphabet: (1)&nbsp;the interview of one attorney at Cravath regarding the SLC&#146;s process and independence; and (2)&nbsp;the review of over 5,300 additional pages of relevant documents made available to Settling
Stockholders&#146; Counsel by Alphabet. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">37.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;As to the legal merits of the
claims asserted in the Settled Matters, the Settling Parties have expended significant time and resources participating in a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">two-day</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-person</FONT> mediation and <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-</FONT> and post-mediation conference calls and working group meetings, where the merits of the claims asserted in the Settled Maters and defenses thereto were extensively discussed between the parties and
independently with the mediator, Judge Kleinberg. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">38.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;After considerable
review and deliberation, the SLC approved the terms and conditions in the MOU and the Stipulation, and determined that the Settlement is in the best interests of the Company and its stockholders. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">39.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Settling Parties entered into the Stipulation on August&nbsp;20, 2020.
Prior to signing the Stipulation, the Settling Parties had no negotiations regarding the amount of any Fee&nbsp;&amp; Expense Awards or the amount of any Service Awards. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">40.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On October&nbsp;22, 2020, the California State Court entered the
Preliminary Approval Order in connection with the Settlement which, among other things, preliminarily approved the Settlement, authorized this Notice to be provided to current Alphabet stockholders, and scheduled the Settlement Hearing to consider
whether to grant final approval of the Settlement. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P><DIV ALIGN="right">
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="99%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">


<TR>

<TD WIDTH="100%"></TD></TR>


<TR STYLE="font-size:1pt">
<TD HEIGHT="8" STYLE="BORDER-LEFT:1px solid #000000; BORDER-TOP:1px solid #000000; BORDER-RIGHT:1px solid #000000; padding-left:8pt" BGCOLOR="#e6e6e6">&nbsp;</TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">
<TD VALIGN="bottom" ALIGN="center" STYLE="padding-bottom:6pt ;BORDER-LEFT:1px solid #000000; BORDER-RIGHT:1px solid #000000; BORDER-BOTTOM:1px solid #000000; padding-left:8pt; padding-right:2pt" BGCOLOR="#e6e6e6">WHAT ARE THE TERMS OF THE
SETTLEMENT?</TD></TR>
</TABLE></DIV> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">41.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In consideration of the Settlement
and the releases provided therein, and subject to the terms and conditions of the Stipulation, the Settling Parties have agreed to the following Settlement Consideration for Alphabet. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">42.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>Corporate Governance and Workplace Measures and Enhancements.</U>
Alphabet shall adopt and/or maintain (to the extent already implemented) for at least five years a robust program designed to prevent and/or address sexual harassment, sexual misconduct, retaliation, discrimination, and pay equity. These corporate
governance and workplace measures and enhancements are set forth in Paragraph 1.2 of the Stipulation (the &#147;<B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Agreed-To</FONT> Measures</B>&#148;). </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">9 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">43.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>DEI Advisory
Council.</U> Alphabet shall establish and maintain for at least five years a DEI Advisory Council. Membership in the DEI Advisory Council will consist of external and internal members, including Alphabet&#146;s Chief Executive Officer who will serve
on the DEI Advisory Council for the first year. The substantive terms of the DEI Advisory Council are described in Paragraph 1.3 of the Stipulation. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">44.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>Workplace Initiative and Funding Component.</U> Alphabet shall commit
funds to be spent on a set of workplace initiatives and programs (the &#147;<B>Workplace Initiative</B>&#148;). The Workplace Initiative will support a set of global initiatives and programs that focus on the following key areas: (a)&nbsp;expanding
the pool of technologists, especially those who are historically underrepresented (i.e., diverse, historically underrepresented, and/or disadvantaged individuals or groups), including by increasing educational and career opportunities through
investments in computer science programs to build computer science talent; (b)&nbsp;hiring, progression, and retention of historically underrepresented talent at Alphabet and in particular at Google; (c)&nbsp;fostering respectful, equitable, and
inclusive workplace cultures; and (d)&nbsp;helping historically underrepresented groups and individuals succeed with their businesses and in the digital economy and tech industry, including by supporting conferences and events and increasing access
to digital tools and opportunities. The substantive terms of the Workplace Initiative are described in Paragraph 1.4 of the Stipulation. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">45.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In order to provide appropriate funding for the Workplace Initiative,
Alphabet shall cause to be spent a total of $310&nbsp;million over the course of up to 10 years starting the first full fiscal year following the Effective Date of the Settlement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">46.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On November&nbsp;8, 2018, Google, publicly announced a number of workplace
commitments (the &#147;<B>November 2018 Commitments</B>&#148;). The Company shall adopt the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Agreed-To</FONT> Measures in addition to or in conjunction with the November 2018 Commitments, and acknowledges that the
Settling Stockholders and their counsel were a substantial and material factor in the adoption and/or maintenance of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Agreed-To</FONT> Measures. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" ALIGN="center">


<TR>

<TD WIDTH="100%"></TD></TR>


<TR STYLE="font-size:1pt">
<TD HEIGHT="8" STYLE="BORDER-LEFT:1px solid #000000; BORDER-TOP:1px solid #000000; BORDER-RIGHT:1px solid #000000; padding-left:8pt" BGCOLOR="#e6e6e6">&nbsp;</TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">
<TD VALIGN="bottom" ALIGN="center" STYLE="padding-bottom:6pt ;BORDER-LEFT:1px solid #000000; BORDER-RIGHT:1px solid #000000; BORDER-BOTTOM:1px solid #000000; padding-left:8pt; padding-right:2pt" BGCOLOR="#e6e6e6">WHAT ARE THE SETTLING PARTIES&#146;
REASONS FOR THE SETTLEMENT?</TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>A.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify"><B>Why did the Settling Stockholders agree to settle? </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">47.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;As discussed above, Settling Stockholders&#146; Counsel have reviewed and
analyzed confidential, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-public</FONT> internal Company documents. In addition, Settling Stockholders&#146; Counsel have reviewed and analyzed data from many other sources specific to this matter, including, but
not limited to: (1)&nbsp;Alphabet&#146;s public filings with the SEC, press releases, announcements, transcripts of investor conference calls, and news articles; and (2)&nbsp;securities analyst, business, and financial media reports about Alphabet.
Settling Stockholders&#146; Counsel have also (1)&nbsp;researched the applicable law with respect to the claims asserted (or which could be asserted) in the stockholder derivative actions and the potential defenses thereto; (2)&nbsp;researched,
drafted, and filed complaints or sent litigation and/or inspection demands; (3)&nbsp;consulted with experts retained on numerous matters relevant to the pending litigation and settlement issues; </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">10 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">
(4) prepared detailed mediation statements; (5)&nbsp;reviewed documents and information provided in advance of the mediation sessions and during settlement negotiations, including by counsel to
the SLC, which gave Settling Stockholders&#146; Counsel a detailed presentation of the SLC&#146;s investigation process and findings; (6)&nbsp;consulted with WilmerHale regarding its review of harassment, retaliation, and pay equity policies and
procedures; (7)&nbsp;conducted outreach to significant institutional stockholders of the Company who are not parties to the Settled Matters; (8)&nbsp;participated in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">two-day</FONT>
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-person</FONT> mediation and several working-group meetings; and (9)&nbsp;engaged in months-long settlement discussions with Defendants&#146; counsel. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">48.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Settling Stockholders&#146; Counsel believe that the claims asserted in the
Litigations have merit and that their investigation of the evidence supports the claims asserted. Without conceding the merit of any of the Defendants&#146; defenses, and in light of the benefits of the Settlement as well as to avoid the potentially
protracted time, expense, and uncertainty associated with continued litigation, including potential trial(s) and appeal(s), Settling Stockholders and Settling Stockholders&#146; Counsel have concluded that it is desirable that the Litigations be
fully and finally settled in the manner and upon the terms and conditions set forth in the Stipulation. Settling Stockholders and Settling Stockholders&#146; Counsel recognize the significant risk, expense, and length of continued proceedings
necessary to prosecute the Litigations against Defendants through trial(s) and through possible appeal(s). Settling Stockholders&#146; Counsel have also taken into account the uncertain outcome and the risk of any litigation, especially complex
litigation such as the Litigations, the difficulties and delays inherent in such litigation, the cost to Alphabet&#151;on behalf of which Settling Stockholders filed the Litigations or made Demands&#151;and distraction to management of Alphabet that
would result from extended litigation. Based on their evaluation, and in light of what Settling Stockholders&#146; Counsel believe to be the significant benefits conferred upon Alphabet as a result of the Settlement, Settling Stockholders and
Settling Stockholders&#146; Counsel have determined that the Settlement is in the best interests of Settling Stockholders and Alphabet and have agreed to settle the Litigations upon the terms and subject to the conditions set forth in the
Stipulation. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">49.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition, Judge Kleinberg&#151;the mediator who
presided over the parties&#146; extensive <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-person</FONT> as well as telephonic mediation efforts&#151;concluded that the negotiations were robust and conducted at arms&#146;-length. Through his involvement, Judge
Kleinberg has become intimately familiar with the claims at issue in this case, as well as the risks to all parties of continuing to litigate the claims. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>B.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify"><B>Why did the Settling Defendants and the Company agree to settle? </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">50.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each Individual Defendant has denied and continues to deny that he or she
has committed or attempted to commit any violations of law, any breaches of fiduciary duty owed to Alphabet, or any wrongdoing whatsoever, and expressly maintains, that at all relevant times, he or she acted in good faith and in a manner that he or
she reasonably believed to be in the best interests of Alphabet and its stockholders. Defendants further deny that the Settling Stockholders, Alphabet, or its stockholders suffered any damage or were harmed as a result of any act, omission, or
conduct by the Individual Defendants as alleged in the Settled Matters or otherwise. Defendants further assert, among other things, that the Settling Stockholders lack standing to litigate derivatively on behalf of Alphabet because certain of the
Settling Stockholders have not yet pleaded, and cannot properly plead, that a demand on the Board would be futile; and other of the Settling Stockholders have not yet pleaded, and cannot properly plead, that demand on the Board was refused. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">11 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">51.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Alphabet believes that
the Settlement is in the best interests of the Company, its stockholders, and its employees. Defendants are, therefore, entering into the Settlement for its benefits and to eliminate the uncertainty, distraction, disruption, burden, risk, and
expense of further litigation. Pursuant to the terms set forth in the Stipulation, neither the Stipulation (including the exhibits) nor any Fee Agreement shall in any event be construed as, or deemed to be evidence of, an admission or concession by
the Individual Defendants with respect to any claim of fault, liability, wrongdoing, or damage or any defect in the defenses that Individual Defendants have, or could have, asserted. Each Individual Defendant has further asserted, and continues to
assert, that at all material times, the Individual Defendant acted in good faith and in a manner that she or he reasonably believed to be in the best interests of Alphabet and its stockholders. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>C.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify"><B>What is the Special Litigation Committee&#146;s position? </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">52.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;After deliberation, the SLC concluded that the terms of the Settlement are
fair and reasonable to Alphabet and that it is in the best interest of the Company and its stockholders to enter into the Stipulation. In reaching that determination, the SLC considered the facts and circumstances surrounding the proposed
settlement, including among other matters: (i)&nbsp;the SLC&#146;s view, based on its thorough investigation, of the strengths and weaknesses in the claims asserted by the Settling Stockholders and the Defendants&#146; anticipated defenses;
(ii)&nbsp;the expense, risks and uncertainties of continued litigation; (iii)&nbsp;the effects, including reputational, on Alphabet and its employees of continued litigation; and (iv)&nbsp;the benefits the Settlement affords the Company and the
desirability of permitting the Settlement to be consummated according to its terms. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P><DIV ALIGN="right">
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="99%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">


<TR>

<TD WIDTH="100%"></TD></TR>


<TR STYLE="font-size:1pt">
<TD HEIGHT="8" STYLE="BORDER-LEFT:1px solid #000000; BORDER-TOP:1px solid #000000; BORDER-RIGHT:1px solid #000000; padding-left:8pt" BGCOLOR="#e6e6e6">&nbsp;</TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">
<TD VALIGN="bottom" ALIGN="center" STYLE="padding-bottom:6pt ;BORDER-LEFT:1px solid #000000; BORDER-RIGHT:1px solid #000000; BORDER-BOTTOM:1px solid #000000; padding-left:8pt; padding-right:2pt" BGCOLOR="#e6e6e6">WHAT WILL HAPPEN IF THE SETTLEMENT
IS APPROVED?<BR>WHAT CLAIMS WILL THE SETTLEMENT RELEASE?</TD></TR>
</TABLE></DIV> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">53.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If the Settlement is approved, the
California State Court will enter a Judgment. Pursuant to the Judgment, the California Action will be dismissed in its entirety and with prejudice and, upon the Effective Date of the Settlement,<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>
the following releases will occur: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">54.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B>Release of Claims by Current
Alphabet Stockholders.</B> Upon the Effective Date, the Settling Stockholders (acting on their own behalf and, in some cases, derivatively on behalf of Alphabet), Alphabet, and any Person acting derivatively on behalf of Alphabet shall be deemed to
have, and by operation of the Judgment shall have, fully, finally, and forever released, relinquished, discharged and dismissed with prejudice the Released Stockholder Claims which, as detailed in the Stipulation, means any and all claims, rights,
demands, obligations, controversies, </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="line-height:8.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;width:25%">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP> The Effective Date of the Settlement is conditioned on the occurrence of
each of the events described in Paragraph 6.1 of the Stipulation, which include the entry of the Judgment by the California State Court approving the Settlement and dismissing the California Action<I> </I>with prejudice, the dismissal with prejudice
of the other related Litigations, the withdrawal of the Demands, the passing of the date upon which the Judgment becomes Final, and the passing of the dates upon which each of the dismissal orders in the Litigations become Final. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">12 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">
debts, disputes, damages, losses, actions, causes of action, sums of money due, judgments, suits, amounts, matters, issues, liabilities, and charges of any kind or nature whatsoever (including,
but not limited to, any claims for interest, attorneys&#146; fees, expert or consulting fees, and any other costs, expenses, amounts, or liabilities whatsoever), and claims for relief of every nature and description whatsoever, whether in law or
equity, including both known claims and Unknown Claims (as defined in Paragraph I(kk) of the Stipulation), suspected or unsuspected, accrued or unaccrued, fixed or contingent, liquidated or unliquidated, matured or unmatured, foreseen or unforeseen,
whether arising under federal or state statutory or common law, or any other law, rule, or regulation, whether foreign or domestic, that Alphabet, the Settling Stockholders derivatively on behalf of Alphabet, or any Alphabet stockholder derivatively
on behalf of Alphabet (i)&nbsp;asserted in any of the complaints filed in the Litigations or in the Demands in the Settled Matters, or (ii)&nbsp;could have asserted in any court, tribunal, forum, or proceeding, arising out of, relating to, or based
upon the facts, allegations, events, disclosures, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-disclosures,</FONT> occurrences, representations, statements, matters, transactions, conduct, actions, failures to act, omissions, or circumstances that were
alleged or referred to in any of the complaints filed in the Litigations or in the Demands in the Settled Matters against the Released Defendant Persons.<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">4</SUP><SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top"> </SUP>In addition, upon the Effective Date, the Settling Stockholders (acting on their own behalf and, in some cases, derivatively on behalf of Alphabet), Alphabet, and any Person acting derivatively on
behalf of Alphabet, shall be forever barred and enjoined from asserting, commencing, instituting, or prosecuting any of the Released Stockholder Claims against any Released Defendant Persons. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">55.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B>Release of Claims by Defendants. </B>Upon the Effective Date, each of
the Individual Defendants and Alphabet shall be deemed to have, and by operation of the Judgment shall have, fully, finally, and forever released, relinquished, and discharged the Released Defendant Claims which, as detailed in the Stipulation,
means any and all claims, rights, demands, obligations, controversies, debts, damages, losses, causes of action, and liabilities of any kind or nature whatsoever, whether in law or equity, including both known claims and Unknown Claims (as defined
in Paragraph I(kk) of the Stipulation), suspected or unsuspected, accrued or unaccrued, that Defendants have or could have asserted against the Released Stockholder Persons or their counsel, arising out of the institution, prosecution, or settlement
of the claims asserted against Defendants in the Settled Matters that Defendants (i)&nbsp;asserted in the Settled Matters, or (ii)&nbsp;could have asserted in the Settled Matters, or in any other forum that arise out of, relate to, or are based
upon, any of the allegations, transactions, facts, matters, events, disclosures, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-disclosures,</FONT> occurrences, representations, statements, acts or omissions, alleged or referred to in any of the complaints
filed in the Settled Matters against the Released Stockholder Persons and shall be forever barred and enjoined from asserting any Released Defendant Claims against any Released Stockholder
Persons.<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">5</SUP> </P> <P STYLE="font-size:60pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="line-height:8.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;width:25%">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">4</SUP> The Released Stockholder Claims shall not include (i)&nbsp;any claims asserted in the pending stockholder and consumer class actions captioned <I>In re Alphabet, Inc. Securities Litigation</I>, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">4:18-cv-6245-JSW</FONT></FONT></FONT> (N.D. Cal.), and <I>In re Google Plus Profile Litig.</I>, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">5:18-cv-6164-EJD</FONT></FONT></FONT> (N.D. Cal.), (ii) any claims relating to the enforcement of the Settlement or the Stipulation, or (iii)&nbsp;any claims that arise out of or are based
upon any conduct of the Released Defendant Persons after the Effective Date. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">5</SUP> The Released Defendant Claims shall not include (i) any claims relating
to the enforcement of the Settlement or the Stipulation, (ii) any claims by the Individual Defendants relating to insurance coverage or the right to indemnification, or (iii) any claims that arise out of or are based upon any conduct of the Released
Stockholder Persons after the Effective Date. The definition of "Released Defendant Claims" specifically excludes claims in the pending stockholder and consumer class action lawsuits captioned <I>In re Alphabet, Inc. Securities Litigation</I>,
4:18-cv-06245-JSW (N.D. Cal.) and <I>In re Google Plus</I> <I>Profile Litigation</I>, 5:18-cv-06164-EJD (N.D. Cal.). The Stipulation does not release claims in those actions. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">13 </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">56.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;By Order of the
California State Court, pending final determination of whether the Settlement should be approved, the Settling Stockholders and all other current Alphabet stockholders are barred and enjoined from asserting, commencing, instituting, or prosecuting
any of the Released Stockholder Claims against any of the Released Defendant Persons. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">57.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B>THE ABOVE DESCRIPTION OF THE PROPOSED RELEASES IS ONLY A SUMMARY. The
complete terms&#151;including the definitions of the Effective Date, Released Defendant Claims, Released Defendant Persons, Released Stockholder Claims, Released Stockholder Persons, and Unknown Claims&#151;are set forth in the Stipulation</B>,
which is available on Alphabet&#146;s investor relations website at <FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" COLOR="#0000ff"><U>https://abc.xyz/investor/</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman"> and on Plaintiffs&#146; <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Counsel&#146;s websites at </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" COLOR="#0000ff"><U>https://www.bottinilaw.com</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman"> and </FONT><FONT
