ATTORNEYS BE PAID?</TD></TR>
</TABLE></DIV> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">58.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Settling Stockholders&#146; Counsel
have not received any payment for their services in pursuing the claims asserted in the California Action and other Settled Matters, nor have the Settling Stockholders&#146; Counsel been reimbursed for their litigation expenses. In light of benefits
produced for Alphabet by the Settling Stockholders and the Settling Stockholders&#146; Counsel in connection with the Settlement and the Litigations and Demands leading up to it, Plaintiffs&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT>
Counsel intend to seek approval from the California State Court for a Fee&nbsp;&amp; Expense Award not to exceed $29,000,000.00 for attorneys&#146; fees and litigation expenses incurred by the Settling Stockholders&#146; Counsel (other than Delaware
Counsel), an amount negotiated by the Plaintiffs&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Counsel and Defendants&#146; counsel with the assistance of the mediator, the Hon. Layn R. Phillips (Ret.), as memorialized in a Fee Agreement. In
light of the benefits being produced for Alphabet by Irving Fire and Delaware Counsel, Delaware Counsel intends to submit to the Delaware Court a separate petition for a Fee&nbsp;&amp; Expense Award not to exceed $11,330,000.00 for attorneys&#146;
fees and litigation expenses incurred by Delaware Counsel, in an amount negotiated by Delaware Counsel and Defendants&#146; counsel, with the assistance of Judge Phillips, as memorialized in a Fee Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">59.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The California State Court will determine the amount of the Fee&nbsp;&amp;
Expense Award for all Settling Stockholders&#146; Counsel except for Delaware Counsel. The application for a Fee&nbsp;&amp; Expense Award for Delaware Counsel will be separately considered by the Delaware Court and, if approved, shall be paid
separately, and in addition to, any Fee&nbsp;&amp; Expense Award awarded by the California State Court. Alphabet agrees that, to the extent available, it will cause insurance </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">14 </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">
proceeds from the Defendants&#146; insurers to pay for the Fee&nbsp;&amp; Expense Awards in excess of any applicable self-insured retention. Alphabet stockholders are not personally liable for
any such fees or expenses. Any fees and expenses approved by the Court will not diminish or have any impact on the $310&nbsp;million funding commitment by Alphabet pursuant to the Settlement (<I>see </I>Paragraph 45 above). </P>

HEARING BE HELD?<BR>DO I HAVE THE RIGHT TO APPEAR AT THE SETTLEMENT HEARING?</TD></TR>
</TABLE></DIV> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">60.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Court will consider the
Settlement, as well as the Settling Stockholders&#146; Counsel&#146;s (other than Delaware Counsel) application for a Fee&nbsp;&amp; Expense Award at the Settlement Hearing. The Settlement Hearing will be held before The Honorable Brian C. Walsh, on
November&nbsp;30, 2020, at 1:30 p.m., at the Superior Court of the State of California, County of Santa Clara, Dept. 1, 191 North First Street, San Jose, CA 95113. Due to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> pandemic, hearings before
the judge overseeing the California Action are currently being conducted remotely with the assistance of a third-party service provider, CourtCall. Stockholders who wish to appear at the Settlement Hearing should contact Plaintiffs&#146; <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Counsel to arrange a remote appearance through CourtCall, at least three calendar days before the hearing, if possible. Any CourtCall fees for an appearance by an objecting stockholder shall be paid by
Plaintiffs&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Counsel. At the Settlement Hearing, the Court consider whether the Judgment, substantially in the form of Exhibit D to the Stipulation, should be entered: (a)&nbsp;approving the terms
of the Settlement as fair, reasonable, and adequate; (b)&nbsp;dismissing with prejudice the California Action pursuant to the terms of this Stipulation; and (c)&nbsp;ruling upon Settling Stockholders&#146; Counsel&#146;s (other than Delaware
Counsel) application for a Fee&nbsp;&amp; Expense Award; and (d)&nbsp;to consider any other matters that may properly be brought before the Court in connection with the Settlement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">61.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Any Alphabet stockholder who held Alphabet stock as of 2014 and continues
to hold such shares of Alphabet common stock as of the date of the Settlement Hearing may enter an appearance in the Action, at his, her, or its own expense, individually or through counsel of his, her, or its own choice, by filing with the Clerk of
the Court and delivering a notice of appearance to Plaintiffs&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Counsel and to Benjamin M. Crosson of Wilson Sonsini Goodrich&nbsp;&amp; Rosati, P.C. (&#147;<B>Representative Defendants&#146;
Counsel</B>&#148;) and Rachel G. Skaistis of Cravath, Swaine&nbsp;&amp; Moore LLP (&#147;<B>SLC&#146;s Counsel</B>&#148;) at the addresses set forth in Paragraph 63 below, such that it is received no later than ten (10)&nbsp;calendar days prior to
the Settlement Hearing, or as the Court may otherwise direct. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">62.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Any
Alphabet stockholder who held Alphabet stock as of 2014 and continues to hold such shares of Alphabet common stock as of the date of the Settlement Hearing may file a written objection to the proposed Settlement and/or the Settling
Stockholders&#146; Counsel&#146;s (other than Delaware Counsel) application for a Fee&nbsp;&amp; Expense Award, and appear and show cause, if he, she, or it has any cause, why the proposed Settlement and/or the applications for such Fee&nbsp;&amp;
Expense Award should not be approved. All Persons desiring to object are directed to file a written objection with the Clerk of the Court and serve (by hand, first-class mail, or express service) copies of such objection on Plaintiffs&#146; <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Counsel, Representative Defendants&#146; Counsel and the SLC&#146;s Counsel at the addresses set forth below such that they are <B><I>received</I></B> no later than
<B><U>November</U></B><B><U></U></B><B><U>&nbsp;16, 2020</U></B>, which is fourteen (14)&nbsp;calendar days prior to the Settlement Hearing. </P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">63.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Any Alphabet stockholder who held Alphabet
stock as of 2014 and continues to hold shares of Alphabet common stock as of the date of the Settlement Hearing and who wishes to be heard orally at the Settlement Hearing may appear at the hearing, whether or not they have filed an
objection.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">64.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Any Alphabet stockholder who held
Alphabet stock as of 2014 and continues to hold shares of Alphabet common stock as of the date of the Delaware Fee Hearing may file a written objection to Delaware Counsel&#146;s application for a Fee&nbsp;&amp; Expense Award and appear and show
cause, if he, she, or it has any cause, why the application for such Fee&nbsp;&amp; Expense Award should not be approved. All Persons desiring to object are directed to file a written objection with the Register in Chancery and serve (by hand,
first-class mail, or express service) copies of such objection on Delaware Counsel, Lori W. Will of Wilson Sonsini Goodrich&nbsp;&amp; Rosati, P.C. (&#147;<B>Representative Defendants&#146; Delaware Counsel</B>&#148;) and A. Thompson Bayliss of
Abrams&nbsp;&amp; Bayliss LLP (&#147;<B>SLC&#146;s Delaware Counsel</B>&#148;) at the addresses set forth below such that they are <B><I>received</I></B> no later than <B><U>December</U></B><B><U></U></B><B><U>&nbsp;9, 2020</U></B>, which is
fourteen (14)&nbsp;calendar days prior to the Delaware Fee Hearing. </P>

</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">66.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Any objections, filings, and other submissions: (a)&nbsp;must state
the name, address, and telephone number of the objector and, if represented by counsel, the name, address, and telephone number of his, her, or its counsel; (b)&nbsp;must be signed by the objector; (c)&nbsp;must contain a specific, written statement
of the objection(s) and the specific reason(s) for the objection(s), including any legal and evidentiary support the objector wishes to bring to the Court&#146;s or Delaware Court&#146;s attention, and if the objector has indicated that he, she, or
it intends to appear at the Settlement Hearing or Delaware Fee Hearing, the identity of any witnesses the objector may call to testify and any exhibits the objector intends to introduce into evidence at the hearing; and (d)&nbsp;must include
documentation sufficient to prove that the objector owned shares of Alphabet common stock as of 2014 and contain a statement that the objector continues to hold such shares as of the date of filing of the objection and will continue to hold those
shares as of the date of the Settlement Hearing or Delaware Fee Hearing. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">67.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Documentation establishing ownership of Alphabet common stock must consist
of copies of monthly brokerage account statements, or an authorized statement from the objector&#146;s broker containing the information found in an account statement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">68.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;You may file a written objection without having to appear at the Settlement
Hearing or Delaware Fee Hearing. Any current Alphabet stockholder may also appear and object at the Settlement Hearing or Delaware Fee Hearing with or without having submitted a written objection. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">69.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;You are not required to hire an attorney to represent you in making written
objections or in appearing at the Settlement Hearing or Delaware Fee Hearing. However, if you decide to hire an attorney, it will be at your own expense. If you file an objection in connection with or intend to appear at the Settlement Hearing, your
attorney should file a notice of appearance </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">17 </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">70.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Unless the Court (or Delaware Court, as appropriate) orders otherwise, any
Person who does not make his, her, or its objection in the manner provided herein shall: (a)&nbsp;be deemed to have waived and forfeited his, her, or its right to object to any aspect of the proposed Settlement or Fee&nbsp;&amp; Expense Awards;
(b)&nbsp;be forever barred and foreclosed from objecting to the fairness, reasonableness, or adequacy of the Settlement, the Judgment to be entered approving the Settlement, or the Fee&nbsp;&amp; Expense Awards; and (c)&nbsp;be deemed to have waived
